25a5(mdo sde): kho na ste gzhan du ma yin no/ /sha ra dwa ti'i bu gal te 'jig rten gyi khams mtha' yas mu med pa'i gang gA'i klung gi bye ma ji snyed pa de snyed kyi sems can gzhan dag byung bar gyur la/ sa'i khams ji snyed pa dang / chu'i khams ji snyed pa dang / me'i khams ji snyed pa dang / rlung gi khams
25a6(mdo sde): ji snyed pa de snyed kyi sems can gzhan dag byung bar gyur na/ sha ra dwa ti'i bu 'di ji snyam du sems/ sems can de dag mang ba yin nam/ gsol pa/ bcom ldan 'das mang lags so/ /bde bar gshegs pa mang lags so/ /bcom ldan 'das kyis bka' stsal pa/ sha
25a7(mdo sde): ra dwa ti'i bu sems can de dag kyang mngon par shes pa drug dang ldan par gyur te/ re re zhing 'di ltar maud gal gyi bu chen po lta bur rdzu 'phrul dang ldan par gyur la/ rdzu 'phrul can de dag gis 'di ltar sems can de dag ji snyed pa de snyed kyi bdud sdig can mngon par sprul te/ sdig can
25b1(mdo sde): re re la yang sems can de dag ji snyed pa de snyed kyi glang po che'i tshogs yod pa dang / rta'i tshogs dang / shing rta'i tshogs dang / dpung bu chung gi tshogs yod par gyur te/ bgrang ba 'di lta bu'i tshul gyis/ dgra bcom pa rdzu 'phrul can de dag re re sprul pa byed pa'i sprul pa de dag re
25b2(mdo sde): res kyang de bzhin du sprul pa mngon par sprul na/ sha ra dwa ti'i bu 'di ji snyam du sems/ de dag bgrang ba la 'jug par nus sam/ gsol pa/ bcom ldan 'das de ni ma lags so/ /bcom ldan 'das kyis bka' stsal pa/ sems can de dag gis phyir mi ldog pa'i rigs
25b3(mdo sde): kyi bu'am/ rigs kyi bu mo de gang na gnas pa'i stong gsum gyi stong chen po'i 'jig rten gyi khams bsreg par mngon par sprul pa byed na/ sha ra dwa ti'i bu 'di ji snyam du sems/ ci sems can de dag rdzu 'phrul chen po rnam par ston pa yin nam/ gsol pa/ bcom
25b4(mdo sde): ldan 'das de dag ni rdzu 'phrul che ba lags so/ /rdzu 'phrul chen po dang ldan zhing / 'jigs pa chen po'i tshul gyis nye bar gnas pa lags so/ /bcom ldan 'das kyis bka' stsal pa/ sha ra dwa ti'i bu gal te de dag 'jig rten gyi khams mtha' yas mu med pa gang gA'i
25b5(mdo sde): klung gi bye ma snyed kyi bskal par gnas la/ de ltar 'jigs pa drag po kun nas ston kyang phyir mi ldog pa'i byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po de dag gi sems zad par bya ba'am/ zil gyis mnan pa'am/ bzlog nus pa'i skal ba med do/ /sha ra dwa ti'i bu 'di ji snyam
25b6(mdo sde): du sems/ sems can dpag tu med pa de dag dang / bdud sdig can de dag gi rdzu 'phrul gang yin pa dang / phyir mi ldog pa'i byang chub sems dpa'i rdzu 'phrul gang yin pa 'di gnyis la/ gang ches mthu dang ldan pa yin/ gsol pa/ bcom ldan 'das rdzu 'phrul dang ldan
25b7(mdo sde): pa 'di dag gi nang na/ phyir mi ldog pa'i byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po'i rdzu 'phrul dang / sems 'di ni ches mthu dang ldan pa lags so/ /bcom ldan 'das kyis bka' stsal pa/ sha ra dwa ti'i bu 'di ji snyam du sems/ 'di lta bu'i rdzu 'phrul dang / stobs dang
26a1(mdo sde): ldan pa gang yin pa de mchog byed pa'am/ mchog tu 'byung bar 'os pa yin nam/ gsol pa/ bcom ldan 'das kyis bka' stsal pa'i don bdag gis 'tshal ba ltar na/ rnam grangs 'dis na thams cad mkhyen pa nyid kyi sems ma gtogs par byang chub sems
26a2(mdo sde): dpa'i sems mchog ces bgyi ba nas gong na ma mchis pa zhes bgyi ba'i bar du ste/ de ci'i slad du zhe na/ phyir mi ldog pa'i byang chub sems dpa'i sems ni zad par bgyir rngo mi thogs pa'i slad du lags so/ /de nas bcom ldan 'das kyis tshe dang ldan pa sha ra dwa ti'i bu la 'di skad
26a3(mdo sde): ces bka' stsal to/ /sha ra dwa ti'i bu de de bzhin no/ /de de bzhin te/ phyir mi ldog pa'i byang chub sems dpa'i sems ni zad par byar mi nus so/ /sbyin pa'i pha rol tu phyin pa las phyir mi ldog pa'i sa'i le'u ste bdun pa'o// //de nas tshe dang ldan pa byams ma'i bu
26a4(mdo sde): gang pos tshe dang ldan pa sha ra dwa ti'i bu la 'di skad ces smras so/ /tshe dang ldan pa sha ra dwa ti'i bu rnam grangs gang gis na/ phyir mi ldog pa'i byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po'i sems zad par byar mi nus/ smras pa/ tshe dang ldan pa gang po gang gi phyir byang chub sems
26a5(mdo sde): dpa' sems dpa' chen po sbyin pa gang dang gang sbyin pa na de thams cad thams cad mkhyen pa nyid la dmigs nas sbyin par byed de/ de bas na byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po'i sems zad par bya ba'am/ zil gyis mnan par mi nus so/ /tshe dang ldan pa gang po dper na/
26a6(mdo sde): skyes bu tshong pa zhig zong 'bum phrag mang po spyod cing / de tshong byed la/ tshong pa des tshong dpon nam/ ded dpon gang yang rung ba las lo 'bum phrag mang po zhig nas skyin po blangs pa las/ de'i tshong ma rung bar gyur nas/ des rgyal po la bskor te rgyal po'i gan du song ngo / /
26a7(mdo sde): de rgyal po'i dpung des na rgyal pos yongs su bzung ba'i mi de la tshong dpon de dang / ded dpon des tshugs par mi 'gyur ro/ /de ci'i phyir zhe na/ de ltar de dpung dang ldan pa'i phyogs 'di lta ste/ rgyal po'i phyogs dpung dang ldan pa'i phyogs de la rten pa'i phyir ro/ /
26b1(mdo sde): tshe dang ldan pa gang po de bzhin du dang po sems bskyed pa'i byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po'i sems dang / phyir mi ldog pa'i byang chub sems dpa'i sems ni dpung dang ldan pa'i phyogs la rten to/ /de ci'i phyir zhe na/ 'di lta ste/ thams cad mkhyen pa nyid kyi phyogs
26b2(mdo sde): dpung dang ldan pa'i phyogs de la rten pas na/ de nyan thos thams cad kyis zil gyis mnan par mi nus so/ /tshe dang ldan pa gang po dper na/ skyes bu rgyal po la rten pa ni longs spyod zad par gyur kyang / 'on kyang tshugs par mi nus pa de bzhin du/ byang chub sems dpa'
26b3(mdo sde): sems dpa' chen po thams cad mkhyen pa nyid kyi phyogs la rten pa yang / 'di ltar nyan thos thams cad dang / bdud thams cad kyis mi tshugs so/ /smras pa/ tshe dang ldan pa sha ra dwa ti'i bu ji ltar na byang chub sems dpa' nyan thos thams cad kyis tshugs par 'gyur/ smras pa/
26b4(mdo sde): tshe dang ldan pa gang po gal te nyan thos kyi sa'am/ rang sangs rgyas kyis sgrogs shing 'chad pa na/ de'i sems skyed cing bdag kyang de ltar gyur cig ces sems skyed na/ nyan thos rnams kyis tshugs pa yin no/ /gang de'i gtam gyi ro myong bar byed pa dang / de la yang dga'
26b5(mdo sde): bar byed pa'i byang chub sems dpa' ni tshul bzhin ma yin pa yid la byed pa bskyed pa des na tshugs par 'gyur ro/ /smras pa/ tshe dang ldan pa sha ra dwa ti'i bu ci'i phyir na/ de dag la tshul bzhin ma yin pa yid la byed pa zhes bya/ smras pa/ 'di dag byang chub sems dpa' sems
26b6(mdo sde): dpa' chen po'i thams cad mkhyen pa nyid la gegs byed pa yin te/ 'di dag skyed par byed pa ma yin la/ 'di dag ni thams cad mkhyen pa nyid ring bar byed pa yin te/ de bas na 'di dag ni byang chub sems dpa'i tshul bzhin ma yin pa yid la byed pa zhes bya'o/ /tshe dang ldan pa
26b7(mdo sde): gang po dper na/ rnal 'byor pa rnal 'byor spyod pa yang dag pa'i mtha' mngon sum du bya bar 'dod cing / yang dag pa la nges par 'jug par 'dod pa'i 'dod chags dang / zhe sdang dang / gti mug kun tu 'byung ba ni dgra bcom pa nyid ring bar byed pa yin te/ de dag de'i tshul bzhin
27a1(mdo sde): ma yin pa yid la byed pa zhes bya'o/ /tshe dang ldan pa gang po de bzhin du byang chub sems dpa' bla na med pa yang dag par rdzogs pa'i byang chub mngon par rdzogs par 'tshang rgya bar 'dod pa'i thams cad mkhyen pa nyid la yang nyan thos dang ldan pa'am/ rang sangs
27a2(mdo sde): rgyas dang ldan pa'i yid la byed pa rnams gegs byed pa yin te/ yid la byed pa de dag skyed na 'di ltar byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po nyan thos rnams kyis zil gyis non pa yin no/ /smras pa/ tshe dang ldan pa sha ra dwa ti'i bu de lta na byang chub sems dpa' nyan thos
27a3(mdo sde): rnams kyis zil gyis non pa yin te/ gang nyan thos dang ldan pa'am/ rang sangs rgyas dang ldan pa'i yid la byed pa skyed pa de ni byang chub sems dpa' zhes mi bya'o/ /de ci'i phyir zhe na/ yid la byed pa de dag gis byang chub sems dpa' zhes bya ba'i grangs su mi chud pa'i phyir ro/ /
27a4(mdo sde): tshe dang ldan pa sha ra dwa ti'i bu dper na/ rgyun du zhugs pa nyon mongs pa kun tu spyod na sbyin gnas su mi 'gyur te/ gal te gang gis de'i nyon mongs pa rnams spong ba'i shes pa thob na/ des de rgyun du zhugs pa zhes bya bar rab tu phye ba yin gyi/ nyon mongs pa rnams kyis
27a5(mdo sde): rab tu phye ba ma yin te/ de ltar na shes pa yongs su shes pa dang / spong ba la 'dris pas de rgyun du zhugs pa zhes bya'o/ /tshe dang ldan pa sha ra dwa ti'i bu de bzhin du byang chub sems dpa' nyan thos dang ldan pa'am/ rang sangs rgyas dang ldan pa'i sems kun tu spyod cing skye bas/ byang
27a6(mdo sde): chub sems dpa' zhes rab tu phye ba ma yin gyi/ thams cad mkhyen pa nyid las brtsams pa'i sems dang sems las byung ba gang dag yin pa de dag skye bas/ 'di lta ste/ de byang chub sems dpa' zhes bya bar rab tu phye ba yin te/ byang chub sems dpa' byang chub kyi sems

27b1(mdo sde): chub sems dpa' byang chub kyi sems la gnas pa yang tshugs par dka'o/ /nyan thos kyi spyod pa'am/ rang sangs rgyas kyi spyod pa thos na yang 'di ltar bdag kyang myur ba nyid du bla na med pa yang dag par rdzogs pa'i byang chub mngon par rdzogs par sangs rgyas nas/ 'di lta ste dper na/

27b4(mdo sde): skyed do/ /tshe dang ldan pa sha ra dwa ti'i bu de ltar na/ byang chub sems dpa' byang chub kyi sems la gnas pa ni thub par dka' ba yin no/ /tshe dang ldan pa dper na/ rnal 'byor pa rnal 'byor spyod pa dmigs pa thob cing / ting nge 'dzin legs par bsgoms pa'i phyir rnam par rtog

27b6(mdo sde): phyir ro/ /smras pa/ tshe dang ldan pa gang po gal te byang chub sems dpa' thub par dka' bar rig par bya na/ theg pa la gsar du zhugs pa gang dag yin pa rnams dang / phyir mi ldog pa gang dag yin pa rnams dang / byang chub kyi snying po la 'dug pa gang dag yin pa thams cad
27b7(mdo sde): dam/ smras pa/ tshe dang ldan pa sha ra dwa ti'i bu byang chub sems dpa' de dag kyang thub par dka' ba yin no/ /de ci'i phyir zhe na/ byang chub sems dpa' de dag dam bcas pa las bskyod mi nus te/ de ltar na byang chub sems dpa' dam bcas pa la gnas pa dang / byang chub kyi
28a1(mdo sde): sems la gnas pa de dag ni thams cad kyang thub par dka' ba yin no/ /tshe dang ldan pa sha ra dwa ti'i bu dper na/ byang chub sems dpa' da ltar mngon par rdzogs par sangs rgyas pa gang yin pa dang / de bzhin gshegs pa lo bye ba brgya phrag mang po nas mngon par

28a6(mdo sde): can yin par rig par bya'o/ /smras pa/ tshe dang ldan pa sha ra dwa ti'i bu de bzhin du byang chub sems dpa' byang chub sems dpa'i sems las phyir ldog pa gang yin pa de ni byang chub tu khas 'che bar zad de/ de ni byang chub sems dpa' ma yin gyi/ de ni byang chub sems dpa'
28a7(mdo sde): sun 'byin pa yin te/ de ni byang chub sems dpa' zhes bya bar rig par bya ba ma yin no/ /smras pa/ tshe dang ldan pa gang po de de bzhin no/ /de de bzhin te/ tshe dang ldan pa gang po dper na/ mi zhig pho mtshan dang ldan par gyur te/ dbang po ma tshang ba ma yin pa las/
28b1(mdo sde): phyis de'i pho mtshan med par gyur la/ pho mtshan gyi bya ba byed mi nus na/ de ni ma ning zhes bya ba'i grangs su 'gro'o/ /tshe dang ldan pa gang po de bzhin du/ byang chub sems dpa'i sems rmug pa ni byang chub sems dpa' zhes bya ba'i grangs su mi 'gro'o/ /sbyin pa'i pha rol tu phyin pa las

28b4(mdo sde): pa'i byang chub sems dpa' ni sbyin pa gang dang gang sbyin pa de thams cad thams cad mkhyen pa nyid du yongs su sngo bar byed do/ /thams cad mkhyen pa nyid du yongs su bsngo na/ sbyin pa'i pha rol tu phyin pa yongs su 'dzin to/ /gal te de ltar yongs su sngo bar mi byed na/ de ni sbyin pa yin gyi/

28b7(mdo sde): dag ni byang chub sems dpa'i thams cad mkhyen pa nyid la bar chad byed pa yin no/ /de ltar rnam par rtog pa ni yun ring mo zhig gis thams cad mkhyen pa nyid thob par 'gyur ro/ /bdag yun ring mo zhig gis thams cad mkhyen pa nyid thob par mi 'gyur grang zhes rnam par rtog

29a4(mdo sde): gang gA'i klung gi bye ma snyed la zan byin la/ de bzhin du sbyin pa yang byin te/ bskal pa gang gA'i klung gi bye ma snyed du gnas shing / de bzhin du yongs su gtong yang ji ltar thams cad mkhyen pa nyid du yongs su bsngo bar bya ba mi shes na/ de ni sbyin pa yin gyi/ sbyin pa'i pha rol tu phyin pa

29a7(mdo sde): pa'i pha rol tu phyin par 'gyur ro/ /tshe dang ldan pa gang po de ltar byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen pos tshad nges pa ma yin pa'i sbyin pa sbyin par bya'o/ /de nas phyis kyang yongs su gtang bar bya'o zhes de ltar yongs su gtang bar bya ste/ byang chub sems dpa' de ni thabs

29b2(mdo sde): bla na med pa yang dag par rdzogs pa'i byang chub mngon par rdzogs par sangs rgyas nas kyang zang zing med pa'i chos kyi sbyin pas sems can rnams la phan gdags par bya'o/ /da ltar ni ji srid du byang chub tu spyod pa'i bar du zang zing gis phan gdags par bya'o/ /bla na med pa yang dag par
29b3(mdo sde): rdzogs pa'i byang chub mngon par rdzogs par sangs rgyas pa na ni/ zang zing med pa'i chos kyi sbyin pas/ sems can rnams la phan gdags par bya'o snyam du sems skyed do/ /tshe dang ldan pa gang po dper na/ mi zhig rgyal po la sten te/ de rgyal po la sten cing 'khor la bsnyen bkur
29b4(mdo sde): byas pas/ rgyal po des de la zan sbyin zhing / des zang zing gi sbyin pas phan 'dogs te/ des bsten cing bskor te/ bsnyen bkur byas pas rgyal po mnyes shing dgyes par gyur nas/ rin po che brgya stong du ma bskon pa de bzhin du/ tshe dang ldan pa gang po byang chub sems dpa' bla na
29b5(mdo sde): med pa yang dag par rdzogs pa'i byang chub tu mngon par rdzogs par 'tshang rgya bar 'dod pas kyang / byang chub tu spyod pa na/ sems can dpag tu med pa la zang zing gi sbyin pas phan 'dogs shing / bla na med pa yang dag par rdzogs pa'i byang chub mngon par rdzogs par sangs rgyas nas kyang /

34b2(mdo sde): te/ 'di ni byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po'i spyod yul lo/ /gal te byang chub sems dpa' bskal pa gang gA'i klung gi bye ma snyed du khyim na gnas te/ 'dod pa'i yon tan lnga rnams la sten cing longs spyod la/ nyan thos kyi sa'am/ rang sangs rgyas kyi sar yang

35a1(mdo sde): pa mtha' yas par mtshams sbyar zhing 'khor bar byas la/ thams cad mkhyen pa nyid kyi sems bskyed de/ thams cad mkhyen pa nyid thob par bya'o snyam du sems bskyed par bya'o/ /de nas tshe dang ldan pa byams ma'i bu gang pos/ tshe dang ldan pa sha ra dwa ti'i bu la 'di skad ces smras

35b7(mdo sde): ris rnams kyis kyang glags mi rnyed do/ /tshe dang ldan pa gang po de ltar na byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po ji lta ji ltar shin tu yun ring por mtshams sbyor ba de lta de ltar sangs rgyas rnams dang / 'phags pa nyan thos rnams dang phrad pa 'thob par 'gyur ro/ /ji lta ji ltar sangs

36a4(mdo sde): gyis non par 'gyur ro/ /gal te nyan thos kyi theg pa pa'i gang zag gis byang chub sems dpa'i theg pa pa'i gang zag tshul khrims kyi pha rol tu phyin pa la rab tu 'doms la/ btams pa'i sems bskyed pa de dag thams cad mkhyen pa nyid du yongs su sngo na/ nyan thos kyi theg pa pa'i gang

39a1(mdo sde): mngon par bsgrub par bya'o/ /rdzu 'phrul des kyang sems can rnams kyi sems kyi spyod pa la 'jug cing shes par bya'o/ /de nas snod du gyur par bya'o snyam ste/ sems kyi khyad par de dag thams cad kyang thams cad mkhyen pa nyid du yongs su sngo na/ byang chub
39a2(mdo sde): sems dpa' tshul khrims dang ldan pa yin par rig par bya'o/ /tshe dang ldan pa gang po gzhan yang byang chub sems dpa' shes rab gang dang gang la spyod cing / phung po la mkhas pa'am/ khams la mkhas pa'am/ skye mched la mkhas pa'am/ rten cing 'brel par 'byung
39a3(mdo sde): ba la mkhas pa'am/ gnas dang gnas ma yin pa la mkhas pa'am/ mnyam pa nyid du 'du shes nas 'du shes thams cad spang ba'i phyir chos bstan par bya'o snyam ste/ sems bskyed pa gang yin pa de dag thams cad mkhyen pa nyid du yongs su sngo na/ byang chub sems
39a4(mdo sde): dpa' tshul khrims dang ldan pa yin par rig par bya'o/ /bla na med pa'i tshul khrims dang ldan par rig par bya'o/ /gal te byang chub sems dpa' pha rol tu phyin pa drug thams cad mkhyen pa nyid du yongs su sngo ba'i byang chub sems dpa' de la ni nyan thos gang gis kyang tshul khrims
39a5(mdo sde): kyis zil gyis gnon nus pa gang yang med do/ /tshe dang ldan pa gang po gzhan yang gal te sems can thams cad dge ba bcu'i las kyi lam dang ldan par gyur na/ de dag gi tshul khrims gang yin pa de ni theg pa la dang po zhugs pa'i byang chub sems dpa'i sems dang po bskyed

39a7(mdo sde): chub sems dpa'i sems dang po bskyed pa'i tshul khrims kyi brgya'i char yang nye bar mi 'gro ba nas/ rgyu'i bar du yang nye bar mi 'gro'o/ /tshe dang ldan pa gang po gzhan yang gal te sems can thams cad byams pa la gnas par gyur/ snying rje dang / dga' ba dang / btang snyoms
39b1(mdo sde): la gnas par gyur na/ de dag gi tshul khrims gang yin pa de yang theg pa la dang po zhugs pa'i byang chub sems dpa'i sems dang po bskyed pa'i tshul khrims kyi brgya'i char yang nye bar mi 'gro ba nas/ rgyu'i bar du yang nye bar mi 'gro'o/ /tshe dang ldan pa gang po gzhan yang

39b3(mdo sde): nye bar mi 'gro'o/ /tshe dang ldan pa gang po gzhan yang gal te sems can thams cad mtshan ma med pa'i rjes su 'thun pa'i bzod pa dang ldan par gyur na/ de dag gi tshul khrims gang yin pa de ni theg pa la dang po zhugs pa'i byang chub sems dpa'i sems dang po bskyed pa'i tshul khrims

39b6(mdo sde): zhugs pa'i byang chub sems dpa'i sems dang po bskyed pa'i tshul khrims kyi brgya'i char yang nye bar mi 'gro ba nas rgyu'i bar du yang nye bar mi 'gro'o/ /de nas tshe dang ldan pa byams ma'i bu gang pos tshe dang ldan pa sha ra dwa ti'i bu la 'di skad ces smras so/ /gal te tshe dang ldan pa sha ra
39b7(mdo sde): dwa ti'i bus bdag gi dri ba dris pa lan gdab pa'i skabs phye na/ tshe dang ldan pa la bdag phyogs 'ga' zhig 'dri'o/ /smras pa/ tshe dang ldan pa gang po dris shig dang thos pa'i don brda sprad par bya'o/ /smras pa/ tshe dang ldan pa sha ra dwa ti'i bu ji gzugs brgyad pa yin par 'dod
40a1(mdo sde): dam/ smras pa/ tshe dang ldan pa gang po de ni ma yin no/ /smras pa/ tshor ba dang / 'du shes dang / 'du byed rnams dang / rnam par shes pa brgyad pa yin par 'dod dam/ smras pa/ tshe dang ldan pa gang po de ni ma yin no/ /smras pa/ de las gzhan pa'i chos rnams
40a2(mdo sde): la brgyad par 'dod dam/ smras pa/ tshe dang ldan pa gang po de ni ma yin no/ /smras pa/ tshe dang ldan pa sha ra dwa ti'i bu 'o na brgyad pa de gang yin par 'dod/ bdag gis tshe dang ldan pa sha ra dwa ti'i bus bshad pa'i don de ji lta bur shes par bya/ smras pa/ tshe dang ldan pa gang po chos
40a3(mdo sde): 'di rnams kyi mnyam pa nyid sems can thams cad kyis mi shes pa de la shes pa gang gis mnyam pa nyid de mngon sum du byed pa'i shes pa de ni bya ba byas pa'i phyir thob pa yin te/ de la brgyad pa ni yang dag par rjes su mi mthong ngo / /gal te gnas 'di rnyed na ni mnyam pa nyid shes pa 'di
40a4(mdo sde): la brtag cing brgal ba med do/ /smras pa/ 'di skad du brgyad pa'i tshul khrims gang yin pa de ni byang chub sems dpa'i tshul khrims kyi brgya'i char yang nye bar mi 'gro ba nas/ rgyu'i bar du'ang nye bar mi 'gro'o zhes kyang zer na/ tshe dang ldan pa sha ra dwa ti'i bu 'di la snga ma dang phyi ma

40a6(mdo sde): ltar bstan to/ /ci nas sems can rnams 'jug par 'gyur ba de ltar bstan to/ /ci nas skye bo mang pos go bar 'gyur ba de ltar bstan to/ /ci nas theg pa chen po dang / sangs rgyas kyi theg pa 'bar bar 'gyur ba de ltar bstan to/ /brgyad pa'i tshul khrims gang yin pa de ni
40a7(mdo sde): theg pa la dang po zhugs pa'i byang chub sems dpa'i sems dang po bskyed pa'i tshul khrims kyi brgya'i char yang nye bar mi 'gro ba nas/ rgyu'i bar du yang nye bar mi 'gro'o/ /tshe dang ldan pa gang po gzhan yang rgyun du zhugs pa thams cad dang / /lan cig phyir 'ong ba thams cad dang / phyir

40b2(mdo sde): mi 'gro'o/ /tshe dang ldan pa gang po gzhan yang nyan thos gang byang chub sems dpa'i tshul khrims zil gyis mnan par sems pa de ni/ de bzhin gshegs pa'i tshul khrims zil gyis mnan par 'dod par zad de/ de ni de bzhin gshegs pa dang rtsod par sems su zad do/ /
40b3(mdo sde): tshe dang ldan pa gang po dper na gang rgyal po'i bu dang rtsod par sems pa de ni/ rgyal po dang rtsod par sems par zad do/ /tshe dang ldan pa gang po de bzhin du byang chub sems dpa'i tshul khrims zil gyis mnan par sems pa gang yin pa de ni de bzhin gshegs pa'i tshul khrims zil gyis
40b4(mdo sde): mnan par sems par zad do/ /de ci'i phyir zhe na/ 'di ltar byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po rnams ni thub par dka' ba yin pa'i phyir ro/ /tshe dang ldan pa gang po dper na mi la la zhig rkang lag med par gyur la 'di skad du/ bdag 'di nas rgya mtsho chen po'i pha rol
40b5(mdo sde): gyi 'gram du mchong bar bya'o zhes zer na/ de skad zer ba de la mi de ni mngon pa'i nga rgyal gyis nga rgyal byed de bla bar rig par bya'o/ /tshe dang ldan pa gang po de bzhin du nyan thos sam/ rang sangs rgyas gang 'di skad du/ bdag gis byang chub sems dpa'i tshul khrims zil gyis
40b6(mdo sde): gnan par bya'o zhes zer na/ tshe dang ldan pa gang po 'di ltar de ni bla bar rig par bya'o/ /de ci'i phyir zhe na/ byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po rnams ni rgya mtsho dug can pa dang 'dra ba yin pa'i phyir ro/ /ji ltar mi de rkang lag rnams med bzhin du rgya mtsho la mchong
40b7(mdo sde): bar 'dod pa de bzhin du nyan thos kyi theg pa pa'am/ rang sangs rgyas kyi theg pa pa'i gang zag byang chub sems dpa'i chos rnams med bzhin du byang chub sems dpa'i tshul khrims zil gyis non par 'gyur ba de ni gnas med do/ /de ci'i phyir zhe na/ byang chub sems dpa'
41a1(mdo sde): sems dpa' chen po rnams ni tshul khrims dpag tu med pa dang ldan pa yin pa'i phyir ro/ /smras pa/ tshe dang ldan pa sha ra dwa ti'i bu ci'i phyir na byang chub sems dpa' rnams tshul khrims dpag tu med pa dang ldan pa yin/ smras pa/ tshe dang ldan pa gang po sems can
41a2(mdo sde): tshul khrims 'chal pa dpag tu med pa dag 'chal pa'i tshul khrims las yongs su dgrol bar 'dod pa dang / tshul khrims la dgod par 'dod pa'i phyir ro/ /smras pa/ tshe dang ldan pa sha ra dwa ti'i bu 'di lta ste/ 'chal pa'i tshul khrims zhes bya ba de gang gi tshig / smras
41a3(mdo sde): pa/ 'di lta ste/ 'chal pa'i tshul khrims zhes bya ba ni ngar 'dzin pa dang / nga yir 'dzin pa dang / dmigs pa'i 'du shes dang / sems can du 'du shes pa dang / srog tu 'du shes pa dang / gang zag tu 'du shes pa dang / yod par 'du shes pa dang / med par 'du shes pa'i

41a5(mdo sde): dpag tu med pa dang ldan pa de ni nyan thos rnams sam/ rang sangs rgyas rnams kyis zil gyis mnan par sla ba ma yin no/ /byang chub sems dpa' ni 'di lta ste/ tshul khrims kyi pha rol tu phyin pa thams cad mkhyen pa nyid du yongs su bsngo ba'i phyir ming tsam gyis kyang nyan thos

41a7(mdo sde): khrims ni bdag nyid la phan pa'i phyir bskyed pa yin la/ byang chub sems dpa'i tshul khrims ni sems can dpag tu med pa rnams kyi ched du yongs su bsngos pa yin te/ de ltar na byang chub sems dpa'i tshul khrims kyis zag pa med pa'i tshul khrims zil gyis gnon to/ /tshe
41b1(mdo sde): dang ldan pa gang po gzhan yang gal te byang chub sems dpa'i tshul khrims tshad nges pa zhig sgrub tu zin na ni/ zag pa med pa'i tshul khrims kyang zil gyis gnon par mi 'gyur la/ de'i tshul khrims kyang pha rol tu phyin par mi 'gyur ba zhig na/ gang gi phyir sems can dpag tu

41b3(mdo sde): gyis gnon to/ /tshe dang ldan pa gang po de bzhin du byang chub sems dpa'i tshul khrims thams cad mkhyen pa nyid du yongs su bsngos pas kyang gzhan mu stegs can spyod pa pa dang / kun tu rgyu dang / gcer bu pa la sogs pa nas 'phags pa nyan thos dang / rang sangs rgyas kyi bar

41b6(mdo sde): yang skyed na/ rang gi spyod yul la spyod pas de'i tshe byang chub sems dpa' tshul khrims kyi pha rol tu phyin pa thob pa yin par rig par bya'o/ /smras pa/ tshe dang ldan pa gang po gang gi tshe byang chub sems dpa' thams cad mkhyen pa nyid kyi sems mi skyed pa de'i tshe byang chub sems
41b7(mdo sde): dpa' la ji skad ces bya/ smras pa/ tshe dang ldan pa gang po de'i tshe byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po sems kyi rgyud lung du ma bstan pa la gnas pa'i tshul khrims dang ldan pa zhes bya'o/ /gal te nyan thos nyid dam/ rang sangs rgyas nyid du yongs su sngo na ni de'i tshe byang chub

43a4(mdo sde): chub sems dpa'i tshul khrims ni de bzhin gshegs pa ma gtogs par zag pa dang bcas pa dang / zag pa med pa'i tshul khrims de dag thams cad kyi mchog ces brjod pa yin zhing gong na med pa zhes bya ba'i bar du brjod pa yin pa'i phyir ro/ /tshul khrims kyi pha rol tu phyin pa
43a5(mdo sde): las le'u gsum pa'o/ / //bam po bzhi pa/ de nas sangs rgyas kyi mthus tshe dang ldan pa sha ra dwa ti'i bus 'di dang nye ba'i 'bum gyi 'jig rten gyi khams na sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das chos ston cing bzhugs pa zhig mthong ngo / /de nas bcom ldan 'das
43a6(mdo sde): kyis tshe dang ldan pa sha ra dwa ti'i bu la bka' stsal pa/ sha ra dwa ti'i bu 'di dang nye ba'i 'bum gyi 'jig rten gyi khams na/ de bzhin gshegs pa zhig chos ston pa khyod kyis mthong ngam/ gsol pa/ bcom ldan 'das mthong lags na/ bcom ldan 'das de ni gang lags/
43a7(mdo sde): 'jig rten gyi khams sangs rgyas kyi zhing de'i ming ni ci zhes bgyi/ bcom ldan 'das kyis bka' stsal pa/ sha ra dwa ti'i bu 'jig rten gyi khams de'i ming ni sgron ma zhes bya'o/ /sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das chos ston pa de'i mtshan ni zla 'od ces bya'o/ /de'i nyan thos rdzu 'phrul
43b1(mdo sde): dang ldan pa mgo zhes bya ba zhig yod de/ des rdzu 'phrul gyis ri'i rgyal po ri rab 'jig rten gyi khams gzhan nas lag pas blangs te/ tshangs pa'i 'jig rten du thug par 'phangs nas de'i bar skabs su byang chub sems dpas tshig 'di skad ces byang chub sems dpa'i tshul khrims

44a1(mdo sde): pa de ni byang chub sems dpa' zhes kyang mi bya'o/ /tshe dang ldan pa gang po dper na gal te 'phong gi slob dpon gyis mda' gzas pa bzhin mi 'gro na de 'phong gi slob dpon zhes mi bya'o/ /tshe dang ldan pa gang po de bzhin du gal te byang chub sems dpa'i sems dang sems
44a2(mdo sde): las byung ba rnams thams cad mkhyen pa nyid dang mi ldan pa 'byung ngam/ yang na sbyin pa sbyin nam/ tshul khrims srung ngam/ bzod pa sgrub bam/ brtson 'grus rtsom mam/ bsam gtan rnams la mnyam par 'jog gam/ shes rab sgom yang rung ste rnam pa thams cad mkhyen

57b1(mdo sde): sangs rgyas kyi sa la 'dod par byed na/ byang chub sems dpas rang gi spyod yul bor te/ gzhan gyi spyod yul la gnas pa yin par yang rig par bya'o/ /smras pa/ tshe dang ldan pa gang po ji tsam gyis na byang chub sems dpa' gzhan gyi spyod yul la spyod pa zhes bya/ smras pa/

99a7(mdo sde): de bzhin mnyen pa ste/ /de ni snyan cing 'jam pa dang / /yid 'ong dga' byed gsal ba ste/ /skyon dang bral zhing 'jigs pa med/ /re ba rnams la char rgyun ltar/ /sems rgyun tshim par byed la zhi/ /ma nyams ma 'khrul rab tu zhi/ /de bzhin dag cing brda phrad sla/ /
99b1(mdo sde): skal dang ldan zhing snyan par ldan/ /don dang yon tan thams cad tshogs/ /gsung gi rgyan rnams phun sum tshogs/ /de yi gsung ni dge skyed pa/ /sems can mos pa tha dad dang / /de bzhin nges tshig tha dad rnams/ /de yi gsung la nges par dad/ /yid kyang
99b2(mdo sde): rab tu dga' bar 'gyur/ /des ni phyogs bcu'i 'jig rten khams/ /gnas pa'i sems can gsung gis khyab/ /mgon po de yi gsung tshig ni/ /sems can rnams la don yod 'jug /thub pa skyes mchog de yi ni/ /mgur yang dung 'dra dpung mgo zlum/ /
99b3(mdo sde): de yi thal gong rgyas pa ste/ /de ni bdun po mtho ba mnga'/ /de yi phyag kyang rab tu ring / /pags pa gser mdog 'dra ba ste/ /gser gyi sdong po bzhin du mtho/ /n+ya gro da ltar chu zheng gab/ /thugs ka dpal gyi be'us brgyan/ /'khor lo'i mtshan can
99b4(mdo sde): pad ma'i phyag / shing bal 'dab ltar reg na 'jam/ /de yi phyag gi sor mo ring / /spu rnams re rer skyes shing yar phyogs stug la 'jam/ /brang gi phel ka che la rab rgyas lte ba zab/ /phyal dbyibs gzhu 'dra glang chen bzhin du sbubs su nub/ /rje ngar e ne ya
99b5(mdo sde): 'dra mdangs dkar 'dam bu'i sbubs/ /long bu mi mngon de yi rting pa legs par grub/ /de bzhin drang srong sor mo ring zhing sen mo dmar/ /bde bar gshegs kyi zhabs kyi long bu mi mngon te/ /'khor lo lcags kyu bkra shis ldan dang dung gis spras/ /mgon po
99b6(mdo sde): de yi zhabs gnyis mnyam zhing legs gnas dang / /shing bal bzhin du reg na 'jam zhing bzang ba dang / /me tog uta pal dmar po legs par skyes pa yi/ /kha dog 'dra bas sa gzhi dag la gshegs par mdzad/ /de bzhin gshegs pa seng ge'i sgra sgrogs

100a1(mdo sde): skar khung 'dir zhog shig dang / de bzhin gshegs pa blta'o/ /de nas ma ma des khye'u rin chen byin skar khung du bzhag go/ /de nas bcom ldan 'das kyis khye'u rin chen byin gyi sems kyi yongs su rtog pa thugs kyis mkhyen nas srang de kho
100a2(mdo sde): nar gshegs so/ /khye'u rin chen byin gyis kyang bcom ldan 'das gshegs pa mthong ngo / /mthong nas kyang de 'di snyam du sems te/ /gang dag de bzhin gshegs pa yon tan thams cad dang ldan pa 'di lta bu mthong nas byang chub kyi sems skyed par mi byed pa de

177b3(mdo sde): gnod sbyin gyi rgyal po'i pho brang dang / dri za'i rgyal po'i pho brang dang / lha ma yin gyi rgyal po'i pho brang dang / nam mkha' lding gi rgyal po'i pho brang dang / mi'am ci'i rgyal po'i pho brang dang / lto 'phye chen po'i rgyal po'i pho brang dang / 'bar ba'i rgyal po'i pho brang dang / sha za'i rgyal po'i
177b4(mdo sde): pho brang de dag tu sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das 'jug pas kyang sangs rgyas kyi mdzad pa mdzad de/ gang 'di grong khyer gyi sgor gshegs nas sa g.yo zhing 'od zer gyi snang bas long ba rnams ni so sor mig thob/ 'on pa rnams ni so sor sgra thos/ smyon pa rnams ni so sor dran pa rnyed/
177b5(mdo sde): gcer bu rnams kyang so sor gos rnyed/ sdug bsngal ba rnams ni so sor bde ba thob/ sil snyan dang brdung ba rnams ma brdungs par yid du 'ong ba'i sgra skad 'byin pa dang / brdung ba ma brdungs pa dang / 'phyang 'phrul rnams 'phyang ba dang / brdungs pa'i sgra dang / bram ze sna
177b6(mdo sde): tshogs mang po rnams kyi sgra skad yid du 'ong ba dang / lta bas mi ngoms shing mi mthun pa med pa gzugs kyi sku ston pas kyang sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das sems can rnams la sangs rgyas kyi mdzad pa mdzad pa dang / mtshan dang dpe byad bstan pas kyang sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das
177b7(mdo sde): sangs rgyas kyi mdzad pa mdzad pa dang / kun tu gzigs pa dang / rnam par gzigs pa dang / brkyang ba dang bskum pas kyang sems can la sangs rgyas kyi mdzad pa mdzad pa dang / mngon par shes pa dang / byon pa dang / bzhengs pa dang / 'chag pa dang / bzhugs pa dang /

178a2(mdo sde): cho 'phrul dang / ston pa'i cho 'phrul dang / rjes su bstan pa'i cho 'phrul gyis kyang sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das sems can rnams la sangs rgyas kyi mdzad pa mdzad pa dang / sna tshogs kyi sems can gyi bsam pa rgya mtsho ma lus pa dang / 'jig rten gyi spyod pa grangs med pa
178a3(mdo sde): thams cad dang / 'jig rten gyi khams kyi yul dang / dge ba'i rtsa ba chen po la gnas pa dang / sangs rgyas dang / sngon gyi gnas rjes su dran pa dang / byang chub sems dpa' dang / yang dag par rdzogs pa'i sangs rgyas kyi gzugs lta bas mi ngoms pa'i phyir 'brang ba dang /
178a4(mdo sde): sangs rgyas rnams 'byung zhing skye ba dang / smra ba dang / de bzhin gshegs pa mthong ba dang / smra ba shin tu dkon pa dang / dkar po'i chos thams cad dang / bsod nams kyi 'byung gnas dang / sangs rgyas mnyes par bya ba dang / de bzhin gshegs pa kha dog mtha'

178a6(mdo sde): ba'i rtsa ba thams cad nye bar spyod pas kyang 'jig rten gyi sems can thams cad la sangs rgyas kyi mdzad pa mdzad pa dang / de dag dang ba dang / phyag 'tshal ba dang / thal mo sbyar ba'i las dang / rjes su ston pa dang / tshig tu 'byin pa dang / yang dang yang du yid la byed pa dang /

179a1(mdo sde): pa na bzhugs pa dang / sku bltar mi snang bar bzhugs pa dang / ye shes zab mo la gnas shing bzhugs pa dang / dpag tu med pa'i sangs rgyas kyi yul gyi stobs la bzhugs pa dang / sku'i spyod pa bltar med pa la bzhugs pa rgyun mi gcod

182a4(mdo sde): thams cad kyi 'jug pa thams cad mngon par mkhyen pa dang / sems can thams cad kyi ngo bo'i ye shes thams cad mngon par mkhyen pa dang / byang chub sems dpa' thams cad kyi dge ba'i rtsa ba chung ngu dang / 'bring dang / chen po dang / sna tshogs rnam par gnas pa'i
182a5(mdo sde): mtshan nyid dang / dge ba'i rtsa ba thams cad dang / bsam pa tshad med pa rgyun mi gcod pa'i mtshams kyi skad cig ma'i ye shes yongs su rdzogs par byed pa thams cad mngon par mkhyen pa dang / chos thams cad rkyen dang 'dus pa tshogs par khong du chud pa thams cad
182a6(mdo sde): mngon par mkhyen pa dang 'jig rten gyi khams thams cad kyi rigs rab tu 'byed pa'i ye shes mthong ba thams cad mngon par mkhyen pa dang / chos kyi dbyings dbye ba mig 'phrul mkhan gyis rnam par phye ba ltar thams cad mngon par mkhyen pa ste/ kye rgyal ba'i sras 'di ni
182a7(mdo sde): sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyis chos thams cad ma lus par mngon par mkhyen pa bcu'o/ /kye rgyal ba'i sras sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi stobs chen po dang / stobs dang / stobs tshad med pa dang / stobs kyi bdag nyid che ba dang / bzod
182b1(mdo sde): par dka' ba'i stobs dang / yongs su ma nyams pa'i stobs dang / snying po'i stobs dang / mi phyed pa'i stobs dang / 'jig rten thams cad kyis bsam gyis mi khyab pa'i stobs dang / sems can thams cad kyis mi 'phrogs pa'i stobs dang / sangs rgyas kyi mthu
182b2(mdo sde): chen po'i stobs kyi dpal gyi chos bcu ste/ bcu gang zhe na/ gang 'di sangs rgyas kyi sku pha rol rgol ba thams cad kyis mi phyed pa dang / 'tsho ba'i dbang po 'jig rten gyi khams thams cad kyis mi chod cing dug gis mi 'jigs pa dang / 'jig rten gyi khams thams cad
182b3(mdo sde): 'tshig pa'i me'i bskal pas mi tshig pa dang / 'jig rten gyi khams thams cad sdud pa dang 'dzin pa'i chu'i phung po'i chus mi 'chi ba dang / bdud thams cad dang / bdud kyi sde thams cad dang / lha thams cad kyi stobs dang / klu thams cad dang / gnod sbyin
182b4(mdo sde): thams cad dang / dri za dang / lha ma yin dang / nam mkha' lding dang / mi'am ci dang / lto 'phye chen po dang / mi dang mi ma yin pa'i stobs dang / sha za dang / 'bar ba thams cad kyi stobs dang / sems can ma lus pa thams cad kyi mig gi stobs kyis mi tshugs
182b5(mdo sde): pa dang / ri rab lhun po'i ri dang mnyam pa'i rdo rje'i char 'bebs pa dang / gzhan yang 'khor yug chen po'i ri dang mnyam pa dang / gzhan yang stong gsum gyi stong chen po'i tshad kyi rdo rje'i char babs te/ des bcom ldan 'das de bzhin gshegs pa dgra bcom pa
182b6(mdo sde): yang dag par rdzogs pa'i sangs rgyas kyi ba spu yang mi 'gul/ bag tsha bar yang mi 'gyur/ bzhud pa dang / bzhengs pa dang / bzhugs pa dang / mnal ba'i spyod lam spang ba'ang mi mnga' ste/ yul gang du de bzhin gshegs pa de ni de bzhin gshegs pa kun tu ji
182b7(mdo sde): tsam du bzhed pa kun tu de tsam du ma bab bo/ /sangs rgyas kyi bsngags pa la yang gtses par ma gyur/ sangs rgyas kyi byin gyis brlabs kyi sems can la yang gtses par ma gyur na de bzhin gshegs pa'i sku mi 'khrugs pa lta ci smos te/ 'di ni sangs rgyas bcom
183a1(mdo sde): ldan 'das rnams kyi mthu chen po'i stobs kyi dpal la gnas pa'i chos dang po'o/ /gzhan yang sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das bzhed na chos thams cad kyi dbyings mchog ma lus pa thams cad dang / 'jig rten gyi khams thams cad dang / ri rab
183a2(mdo sde): lhun po'i ri dang bcas/ kho ra khor yug dang / khor yug chen po'i ri dang bcas/ rgya mtsho'i ri dang nags stug por bcas pa dang / sems can gnas pa'i gnas sna tshogs dang / 'jig rten gyi khams ma lus pa de dag thams cad de bzhin gshegs pa'i ba spu'i
183a3(mdo sde): bu ga gcig tu bcug ste tha ma'i mtha'i bskal pa'i mtha' bzung na/ de bzhin gshegs pa'i byin gyis brlabs ma gtogs par sems can gzhan gyis shes par mi nus so/ /'jig rten gyi khams du ma de dag thams cad de bzhin gshegs pa nyid kyi sku'i ba spu'i bu
183a4(mdo sde): gar bcug nas mtha' ma'i mtha'i bskal par bzung ste/ bzhengs pa dang / bzhud pa dang / bzhugs pa dang / mnal ba dang / bskal par gshegs kyang de bzhin gshegs pa'i thugs la skad cig kyang sdug bsngal du mi 'gyur/ skyo ba mi mnga' ste/ stobs
183a5(mdo sde): dang mthu yongs su nyams par mi 'gyur/ spyod lam la rnam par rtog par mi 'gyur ro/ /kye rgyal ba'i sras 'di lta ste/ dper na nam mkha' ni chos kyi dbyings ma lus pa thams cad dang / 'jig rten gyi khams thams cad 'dzin te/ 'bying ba ma yin/ zhum pa ma
183a6(mdo sde): yin/ 'phel ba ma yin/ 'bri ba ma yin/ 'byung ba ma yin/ skye ba ma yin/ rnam pa ma yin no/ /de bzhin du sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ba spu'i bu ga gcig tu 'jig rten gyi khams ma lus pa thams cad kun 'dzin kyang de'i phyir sdug bsngal tshor ba'i
183a7(mdo sde): sems skye ba gcig kyang mi mnga' ste/ 'di ni sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams sangs rgyas kyi mthu chen po'i stobs kyi dpal la gnas pa'i chos brnyes pa'o/ /gzhan yang sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das gom pa gcig gi spyod pa'i sangs rgyas kyi zhing brjod du med pa'i
183b1(mdo sde): yang brjod du med pa'i rab tu phra ba'i rdul dang mnyam pa'i 'jig rten gyi khams 'dra'o/ /sangs rgyas kyi zhing brjod du med pa'i yang brjod du med pa'i rab tu phra ba'i rdul dang mnyam pa'i bskal par gom pas spyod do/ /du ma'i sems skye zhing 'jug pa de ltar gshegs shing
183b2(mdo sde): 'jig rten gyi khams rab tu phra ba'i rdul dang mnyam pa'i bskal par gshegs te/ 'jig rten gyi khams ma lus pa thams cad du sems bskyed pa bzhin du bskal par gshegs shing 'jig rten gyi khams thams cad kyi rab tu phra ba'i rdul dang mnyam pa'i 'jig rten gyi
183b3(mdo sde): khams kun gnas shing tshad med pa dang / khor yug chen po'i ri brjod du med pa'i yang brjod du med par 'gyur ba dang mnyam pa'i sangs rgyas kyi zhing tha dad pa'i rab tu phra ba'i rdul dang mnyam pa 'das shing ba spu'i bu ga gcig 'gag par 'gyur te/ ji ltar ba spu'i bu ga
183b4(mdo sde): gcig pa de ltar sku'i spu'i bu ga thams cad de sems can thams cad ji snyed pa ba spu'i bu gar gyur la/ de ltar sems can thams cad lci bar gyur la/ sems can de dag thams cad de bzhin gshegs pa'i sor mo gcig gi rtse mos tha ma'i mtha'i bskal par
183b5(mdo sde): 'dzin te/ ji ltar sor mo gcig gis dang por 'dzin pa de ltar sor mo thams cad kyi rtse mos 'dzin kyang de'i phyir de bzhin gshegs pa'i sku bsnyel ba yang mi mnga'/ thugs la skyo bar yang mi 'gyur/ sdug bsngal gyi reg pa tshor ro snyam pa'i sems phra rab gcig tsam
183b6(mdo sde): yang mi skye'o/ /de ltar 'jig rten gyi khams re rer gshegs shing 'jug pa dang / nam mkha' la gshegs shing 'jug pa dang / rgya mo'i phyogs thams cad du gshegs shing 'jug pa dang / de ltar nam mkha'i khams kyi mtha' ma lus pa thams cad dang / chos kyi
183b7(mdo sde): dbyings kyi mthar 'jug pa dang / skra'i rtse mo'i mtha'i tshad kyi khams thams cad du 'jug pa dang / skra rtse re re'i mtha' tshad kyi grangs kyi nam mkha'i khams ma lus pa thams cad yongs su gsol ba'i skra'i rtse mo'i mtha'i tshad kyi nam mkha'i khams su 'jug pa 'dis de bzhin
184a1(mdo sde): gshegs pa'i spyod lam thog ma'i mtha' dang tha ma'i mtha'i bskal par zad cing 'das kyi bar du phyogs dang phyogs na skyil mo krung gcig gis bzhugs shing yongs su longs spyod de/ 'di ni sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi sangs rgyas kyi mthu chen
184a2(mdo sde): po'i stobs kyi dpal la gnas pa'i chos bzhi pa'o/ /gzhan yang sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das sangs rgyas kyi zhing brjod du med pa'i yang brjod du med pa'i rab tu phra ba'i rdul dang mnyam pa'i sku dang dbu du mar gyur la/ dbu gcig la sangs rgyas kyi zhing brjod du med pa'i
184a3(mdo sde): yang brjod du med pa'i rab tu phra ba'i rdul dang mnyam pa'i ljags su gyur pa la sangs rgyas kyi zhing brjod du med pa'i yang brjod du med pa'i rab tu phra ba'i rdul dang mnyam pa'i dbyangs kyi yan lag dang / sgra dang gsung 'jug ste/ chos kyi dbyings ma lus pa thams cad sems can gyi khams la
184a4(mdo sde): go bar byed pa dang / dbyangs kyi yan lag dang / sgra dang / gsung re res kyang sangs rgyas kyi zhing brjod du med pa'i yang brjod du med pa'i rab tu phra ba'i rdul dang mnyam pa'i mdo sde dam pa rab tu bshad la/ mdo sde re re la yang sangs rgyas kyi zhing brjod du med pa'i yang brjod
184a5(mdo sde): du med pa'i rab tu phra ba'i rdul dang mnyam pa'i chos ston pa'i rjes su 'brang la chos bstan pa re re la sangs rgyas kyi zhing brjod du med pa'i yang brjod du med pa'i rab tu phra ba'i rdul dang mnyam pa'i chos kyi tshig dang 'byed pa rnams kyi brjod pa 'gro ste/ ji ltar gang gi phyir chos
184a6(mdo sde): ston pa de ltar chos thams cad ston te/ de dag la sangs rgyas kyi zhing brjod du med pa'i yang brjod du med pa'i rab tu phra ba'i rdul dang mnyam pa'i bskal par ston cing sangs rgyas kyi zhing brjod du med pa'i yang brjod du med pa'i rab tu phra ba'i rdul dang mnyam pa'i bskal pa rnams yongs
184a7(mdo sde): su zad nas yang sangs rgyas kyi zhing brjod du med pa'i yang brjod du med pa'i rab tu phra ba'i rdul dang mnyam pa'i bskal par ston te/ gzhung 'dis 'jig rten gyi khams thams cad kyi rab tu phra ba'i rdul dang mnyam pa'i bskal par ston la/ gzhung 'dis 'jig rten gyi khams
184b1(mdo sde): thams cad kyi rab tu phra ba'i rdul dang mnyam pa'i bskal pa zad pa dang / sems can thams cad kyi sems kyi spyod pa snyed kyi bskal pa zad cing 'das kyang de bzhin gshegs pa'i sprul pa ni de lta ma yin te/ chos thams cad mgal me'i 'khor lo ltar 'jug cing chos thams
184b2(mdo sde): cad shes rab kyis ston te/ brda sprod cing the tsom thams cad gcod pa'i chos kyi 'khor lo skor ba dang / chos thams cad snang bar byed pa'i chos kyi 'khor lo skor ba dang / chags pa med pa'i mdzod kyi 'khor lo skor ba dang / sems can mtha' yas pa tshim par byed pa'i
184b3(mdo sde): 'dul ba'i rgyan gyi chos kyi 'khor lo skor ba dang / byang chub sems dpa'i spyod pa thams cad bsdus pa'i rgyan gyi 'khor lo skor ba dang / ye shes kyi nyi ma'i dkyil 'khor chen po'i rgyun gyi 'khor lo skor ba dang / 'gro ba ma lus pa thams cad la ye shes kyi sgron ma chen po'i rgyun
184b4(mdo sde): gyi 'khor lo skor ba dang / so so yang dag par rig pa dang / mi 'jigs pa chen po'i rgyan gyi chos kyi 'khor lo skor zhing ji ltar sangs rgyas gcig gi sku'i byin gyi brlabs kyis chos kyi 'khor lo skor ba'i sprin chen po yang dpe thams cad kyis dper bya ba ma yin te/ de ltar chos kyi
184b5(mdo sde): dbyings ma lus pa thams cad dang / nam mkha'i khams kyi mthar skra'i rtse mo'i mtha' nas rnam par phye ba chags pa med pa ma lus pa thams cad dang / sangs rgyas kyi zhing brjod du med pa'i yang brjod du med pa'i rab tu phra ba'i rdul dang mnyam pa'i sems kyi skad cig ma dang / sems
184b6(mdo sde): kyi skad cig ma re re de snyed kyi sangs rgyas kyi sprul pa sprul pa dang / ji srid du mtha' ma'i bskal par de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi sprul pa'i sku rnams kyi de bzhin gshegs pa'i sku re re ba de snyed de snyed kyi dbur gyur pa'i bar du sngar kun tu brjod pa bzhin du dbu re re la de snyed de snyed
184b7(mdo sde): kyi ljags su gyur pa'i ljags re re la de snyed de snyed kyi dbyangs kyi yan lag dang / gsung dang / sku dang / gsung 'jug ste/ chos kyi dbyings ma lus pa thams cad sems can gyi khams na go bar byed pa dang / dbyangs kyi yan lag dang / sgra dang / gsung re res de snyed de snyed kyi mdo
185a1(mdo sde): sde rnams 'chad de/ mdo sde re re la de snyed de snyed kyi chos ston pa rjes su 'brang la chos ston pa re re la de snyed de snyed kyi chos kyi tshig dang 'byed pa'i brjod pa 'gro ste/ chos kyi tshig dang 'byed pa re res chos kyi dbyings ma lus pa thams cad sgra gsal bar byed cing sems
185a2(mdo sde): can gyi khams ma lus pa thams cad la go bar byed kyang de bzhin gshegs pa'i gsung 'dzin pa'ang med/ nyams pa'ang med/ zad pa'ang med/ dmas pa'ang med de/ de ltar tha ma'i mthar bskal pa'i bar du gnas shing chos kyi 'khor lo bskor te/ 'di ni sangs rgyas
185a3(mdo sde): bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi sangs rgyas kyi mthu chen po'i stobs kyi dpal la gnas pa'i chos lnga pa'o/ /gzhan yang sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das kyi thugs dpal gyi be'u'i rgyun dang ldan zhing / rdo rje'i snying po chen pos bzung ba de dag byang chub kyi shing drung du gshegs pa
185a4(mdo sde): rnams la bzhag nas sems can thams cad snyed kyis bdud sdig can gyi sde gzugs sna tshogs bskrad cing mi sdug pa/ mchog tu 'jigs pa'i gzugs 'jig rten thams cad 'jigs pa'i gzugs mchog tu sems bskyed pa'i gzugs su 'phrul par byed do/ /byang chub kyi
185a5(mdo sde): shing mchog gi drung du song nas chos thams cad kyi dbyings nam mkha'i mthar bdud kyi mi sdug pa'i gzugs 'dzin pa/ skrag pa chen pos 'jigs pa chen por byed pa/ 'gro ba thams cad 'joms pas/ 'jig rten thams cad 'jig pa'o/ /de na de bzhin gshegs pa byang chub kyi
185a6(mdo sde): shing drung du gshegs nas thams cad la gzigs te/ gzigs nas mi bsnyengs/ bag mi tsha/ spu 'ga' yang mi g.yo/ gzugs sna tshogs kyi mtshan ma sna tshogs 'dzin pa yang mi mnga'/ sems phra mo yang mi mnga' bar gnas te mi g.yo/ mi bskyod mi 'gyur rnam par mi
185a7(mdo sde): rtog / shin tu rab tu zhi/ bsnyengs shing ba spu ldang ba shin tu mi mnga'/ 'dod pa dang khong khro ba shin tu mi mnga'/ sangs rgyas kyi mdzad pa byams pa chen po chags pa med pa'i stobs kyis gtong ba/ dbang po sbed cing thugs rje chen po la gnas pa/ bag mi tsha ba'i thugs dbyer mi
185b1(mdo sde): phyed pa'i snying po thugs mi dang ngas shing zil gyis mi non pa'i thugs kyis bdud dang / bdud kyi ris kyi lha thams cad dang / bdud kyi sde mang po sna tshogs thams cad zil gyis gnon cing gzod nas zil gyis gnon/ bzung nas de bzhin gshegs pa la skyabs su dong ste/ de dag
185b2(mdo sde): la bcom ldan 'das kyis cho 'phrul gsum dang de bzhin gshegs pas 'dul ba bstan te/ bla na med pa yang dag par rdzogs pa'i byang chub las phyir mi ldog par gyur to/ /'di lta ste/ sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi sangs rgyas kyi mthu chen po'i stobs kyi dpal la
185b3(mdo sde): gnas pa'i chos drug pa'o/ /gzhan yang sangs rgyas rnams kyi gsung thogs pa med pas 'jig rten gyi khams ma lus pa thams cad du 'jug cing de dang de dag tu 'jig rten thams cad kyis rnam par rig cing sems can rnams 'dul ba'i dbang gis de bzhin gshegs
185b4(mdo sde): pa'i sgra de ri la thogs pa med de/ ri rab lhun po la mi thogs rin po che'i ri la ma yin/ khor yug dang khor yug chen po la ma yin/ lha'i gnas la ma yin/ klu'i gnas la ma yin/ gnod sbyin gyi gnas la ma yin/ dri za'i gnas la ma yin/ lha ma yin gyi
185b5(mdo sde): gnas la ma yin/ nam mkha' lding gi gnas la ma yin/ mi'am ci'i gnas la ma yin/ mi dang mi ma yin pa'i gnas la lta zhing chags par mi 'gyur ro/ /gal te 'jig rten gyi khams thams cad du gshegs na'ang mi chags te/ 'jig rten srid pa'i khams
185b6(mdo sde): thams cad kyi sgra chen po dang / 'jig rten thams cad kyi sgra sna tshogs rab tu rdzogs pa de la de bzhin gshegs pas brjod pa'i sgras bsgribs par 'gyur te/ ji ltar 'dul ba'i sems can rnams kyi rna bas rnam par rig ste/ gang 'di rna bas rnam par rig cing rnam par rig pa'i
185b7(mdo sde): tshig dang 'byed pa nyams par mi 'gyur te/ de ni 'di ltar de bzhin gshegs pa'i sgra/ lham me/ lhan ne/ lhang nge'o/ /'di ni sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi sangs rgyas kyi mthu chen po'i dpal gyi stobs la gnas pa'i chos kyi sgra bdun pa'o/ /gzhan yang sangs rgyas
186a1(mdo sde): bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi thugs brjod du med pa'i yang brjod du med pa'i bskal pa bye ba khrag khrig brgya stong du shin tu yongs su sbyangs pas chags pa med/ 'das pa dang / ma 'ongs pa dang / da ltar byung ba'i sangs rgyas thams cad kyi rgyan dang zhing rnyog
186a2(mdo sde): pa med pa/ bdag gi med pa'i chos thams cad la gnas pa/ nang dang phyi dang ldan pa ma yin/ ma skyes pa la brtsam pa thams cad rnam par phye ba/ zhi ba/ gnas med pa/ rtsom pa sna tshogs thams cad med pa/ ngo bo thams cad rnam par rtog pa'i 'du shes la gnas
186a3(mdo sde): pa 'gag pa/ rang bzhin 'od gsal ba/ shin tu yongs su dag pa/ rtsom pa dang yid la byed pa thams cad la ma chags pa'i nyon mongs pa med pa'i chos thams cad kyi yul gyi rjes su song ba/ yang dag pa'i mtha' 'dod chags dang bral zhing dag pa/ chos kyi
186a4(mdo sde): dbyings ston pa'i mthar song ba/ chos kyi dbyings kun tu mi zad pa'i rjes su song ba/ 'du shes su gyur pa thams cad dang / tshad dang / tshad med pa dang / 'dus byas dang / 'dus ma byas dang / mngon par smra ba thams cad 'gags pa dag gis lam brjod du med pa'i mtha'i
186a5(mdo sde): yul mi zad cing chags pa med pa'i dbyings kyi mtha'i sngon du ye shes 'gro zhing 'jug pa dang / stobs bcu'i rgyan dang chos thams cad rnam par dag pa/ thabs mkhas pa la zhugs pas chos sna tshogs dang / chos du ma dang / chos thams cad dang / ston pa 'gal ba
186a6(mdo sde): med pa/ dus gsum du dbyer med pa/ chos kyi dbyings thams cad dang / chos thams cad dang / chos thams cad dngos po med pa'i dbang gi pha rol tu song ba/ chos thams cad kyi dbang gi 'byung gnas kyi mdzod kyi khyad par chos thams cad kyi tshul dran zhing kun nas gti
186a7(mdo sde): mug pa zhing thams cad du 'gro ba'i dbang dang / rgya mo'i phyogs ma lus pa thams cad kyi mdo med bcu rdul yab la mi gnas pa/ brtan par gnas shing mi 'pho ba/ ye shes kyi lta ba chos ma lus pa thams cad kyi mthar thug pa/ zag pa thams cad yongs su zad cing zag
186b1(mdo sde): pa med pa/ sems rnam par grol ba/ shes rab rnam par grol ba/ shin tu rnam par grol ba yang dag pa'i mtha' mi zad pa'i mchog chags pa med par gnas pa/ rtag tu mnyam pa dang rab tu ldan pa/ dus gsum la chags pa med par gnas pa/ sems kyi skad cig ma la
186b2(mdo sde): dus gsum gyi sems kyi spyod pa thams cad ma lus par rab tu shes pa ste/ 'di ni sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi mthu chen po'i stobs kyi dpal la gnas pa'i stobs brgyad pa'o/ /gzhan yang sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi chos kyi sgra dang lus gcig
186b3(mdo sde): tu 'dus pa/ sangs rgyas thams cad kyi sku dang yul tshad med pa mtha' dang dbung med pa'i sku yongs su grub pa/ 'jig rten thams cad yongs su 'dzin pa'i sku/ khams gsum gyis mi gos pa'i sku/ rkyen gyi sku rnam par rig cing lhag pa'i bsam pas rjes su dran pa la byin
186b4(mdo sde): gyi brlabs kyi su'i tshogs ston pa/ mi bden mi zhing mnyam pa nyid rnam par dag pa'i sku/ 'ong ba dang / 'gro ba med pa'i chos kyi sku 'dus pa/ 'dus ma byas shing 'jig pa med pa'i sku/ mtshan nyid gcig dang / mtshan nyid med pa'i chos kyi ngo bo nyid kyi sku/ yul na mi
186b5(mdo sde): gnas phyogs na mi gnas pa'i sku/ tshogs ma lus pa thams cad kyi sku/ sangs rgyas khyu mchog rnam par sprul pa'i sku/ kha dog mtha' yas pa'i sku/ sku thams cad rjes su 'brang ba/ sku sna tshogs su rnam par rig pa/ chos kyi sku'i tshul gyi rjes su song ba/ mtha' yas par
186b6(mdo sde): snang ba'i ye shes kyi snying po'i dkyil 'khor gyi mdzod kyi sku/ bya ba sna tshogs med pa/ chos thams cad kyi dbyings ston pa'i sku/ sems can gyi khams ma lus pa thams cad la khyab par gsol ba'i sku 'dus pa/ mi g.yo mi sems pa'i sku rnam par dag pa/ med pa dang med pa ma
186b7(mdo sde): yin pa dang / tshul dang tshul ma yin pas phye ba'i sku/ sems can thams cad kyi dad pa sna tshogs kyi rjes su song zhing 'dul ba'i sku/ 'gags pa dang / 'gags pa ma yin pa 'dul ba la gzigs pa'i yon tan dkon mchog thams cad byung ba bsgreng ba'i sku/ chos thams cad sangs
